data-reactid="1438"><div data-reactid="1439"><div data-reactid="1440">An earth friendly and affordable hostel 5 mi from Clearwater beach and 1 mi from downtown Dunedin.   This is a hostel there are 2 coed beds, 2 male beds and 2 female. The Grimli room is the guys room, The Xena Room is the gals room and Middle Earth is the living room with 2 coed beds in it.  The price is per person.  There is a full kitchen, bathroom &amp; laundry facilities, onsite parking, wifi, dvd library, fire pit, gas grill and free loaner bikes.</div><div data-reactid="1441">This is a shared room with 2 twin beds in it.   All linens are provided. The price is per person.  The other bed is called bed #6 if you are traveling with a friend and want to be in the same room choose that one.  I do not live in the building,  I live next door.  There is always staff on the premises.  Fun, easy going atmosphere.  Homey decor.  This is on the second floor.  

The Nest has six beds total.  2 beds per room.  I have 1 male room, 1 female room and a mixed co-ed room.  In order to do this you might not get the exact bed you see in the pics.  All beds are very similar and all are twins. Two are bunk beds.  This is the only way I can provide separate dorms for the guys and girls.   Sometimes more guys book and sometimes more girls book and I want everyone to be comfortable.   If this is a concern let me know. 

This is my first hostel after being in the vacation rental business for 5 years.  We had a few up and downs in the beginning but now 6 months into it, everything major has been ironed out now.  

Hostels are a great way of traveling inexpensively and connecting with locals and the local community.  Yes, you do have to possess tolerance for lifestyles &amp; beliefs that are different from your own.  In exchange you get built in friends, a support system, advice (albeit sometimes unwanted!) and partners in crime. 

I love seeing guests develop friendships.  Sometimes it's just cooking together or sharing an Uber to the beach.  Many email me and say they still stay in touch with so and so.  What and amazing experience it has been!  

I do try to make everyone as comfortable as possible.  But hosteling is definitely NOT for everyone.  You will run across people you do not care for so much.  You just make the best of it and move on!</div><div data-reactid="1442">A bit of old style Florida tucked away 5 miles from Clearwater Beach and 1 mile from downtown Dunedin.  This two story house built in 1923 is surrounded by organic, tropical, permaculture style gardens. A fun and casual atmosphere our guests often become extended family.  

We are committed to sustainable practices. Onsite composting, recycling, upcycling, rain water harvesting, soil restorations and native wildlife.  The Nest at Sunset House and Gardens is a certified wildlife habitat.  We are home to the endangered Monarch butterfly as well as native birds and plants.

Our rooms feature a homelike environment with 3 full kitchens and 2 kitchenettes,  Bathrooms are cleaned daily with organic detergents.  We provide linens and towels.  Onsite pay per use laundry room.  24 hour onsite staff work hard to make your vacation the best.  The garden has a community patio with gas grill and firepit.  We love music and can often be talked into impromptu drum circles and open jams. 

A little about the garden.  Everything here is organic and edible, medicinal or useful in some way.  My garden does not look like a traditional english style garden because I practice a system/lifestyle called permaculture.  In a nutshell, a permanent culture that renews itself naturally.  Feel free to wander around, use the sitting areas and gas grill. It is not uncommon to see an Egret hunting for his dinner in the garden.  During your stay you are likely to see Oreo, a rescue bunny who lives in the garden.  She is allowed to roam free.  She enjoys human companionship but doesn't like to be picked up or pet. I have ongoing soil restoration projects, rain water harvesting and composting on site.  I'm happy to give garden tours and to gardening tips and advice upon request (to anyone who will listen).</div><div data-reactid="1443"><li data-reactid="1444"><p data-reactid="1445">I love how it was tucked away amongst trees and green.
